def get_prompt(template_name: str, **kwargs) -> str:
    """获取指定模板的提示词"""
    template = CHINESE_PROMPT_TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")
    return template.format(**kwargs)

def validate_chinese_response(response: str) -> bool:
    """验证响应是否为有效中文"""
    if not response:
        return False
    # 检查是否包含中文字符
    chinese_chars = sum(1 for c in response if '\u4e00' <= c <= '\u9fff')
    total_chars = len(response.strip())

代码:
        
        if not source_nodes or not target_nodes:
            return []
        
        paths = []
        # 简化实现：只查找直接路径
        for source in source_nodes:
            for target in target_nodes:
                # 检查直接连接
                for edge in self.graph["edges"]:
                    if edge["source"] == source["id"] and edge["target"] == target["id"]:
                        paths.append([source, {"edge": edge}, target])
        
        return paths

    def run_health_check(self):
        """运行健康检查"""
        status = {}

            health = self.check_agent_health(name)
            status[name] = health
            
            # 自动重启失败的代理
            if health != "running" and self.agents_config[name]["auto_restart"]:
                print(f"[AgentManager] 代理 {name} 状态异常: {health}, 尝试重启...")
                self.restart_agent(name)

    def evaluate_comprehension(self, agent, input_text: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """评估理解能力"""
        response = agent.query_model_chinese(input_text)
        
        # 检查关键词覆盖率
        keywords = [kw for test in self.test_cases if test["input"] == input_text 
                    for kw in test["expected_keywords"]]
        keyword_coverage = sum(1 for kw in keywords if kw in response) / len(keywords)

def get_prompt(template_name: str, **kwargs) -> str:
    """获取指定模板的提示词"""
    template = CHINESE_PROMPT_TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")
    return template.format(**kwargs)

    def evaluate_comprehension(self, agent, input_text: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """评估理解能力"""
        response = agent.query_model_chinese(input_text)
        
        # 检查关键词覆盖率
        keywords = [kw for test in self.test_cases if test["input"] == input_text 
                    for kw in test["expected_keywords"]]
        keyword_coverage = sum(1 for kw in keywords if kw in response) / len(keywords)

代码:
    
    def run_health_check(self):
        """运行健康检查"""
        status = {}
        for name in self.agents_config:
            health = self.check_agent_health(name)
            status[name] = health
            
            # 自动重启失败的代理
            if health != "running" and self.agents_config[name]["auto_restart"]:
                print(f"[AgentManager] 代理 {name} 状态异常: {health}, 尝试重启...")
                self.restart_agent(name)
        
        return status

def get_prompt(template_name: str, **kwargs) -> str:
    """获取指定模板的提示词"""
    template = CHINESE_PROMPT_TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")
    return template.format(**kwargs)

    def stop_agent(self, name):
        """停止单个代理"""
        if name in self.processes:
            proc = self.processes[name]["process"]
            proc.terminate()
            wait_start = time.time()
            while proc.poll() is None and time.time() - wait_start < 5:
                time.sleep(0.5)

    """获取指定模板的提示词"""

def get_prompt(template_name: str, **kwargs) -> str:
    """获取指定模板的提示词"""
    template = CHINESE_PROMPT_TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")
    return template.format(**kwargs)

    def wait_for_login(self, timeout_seconds: int = 120):
        """等待用户手动登录"""
        self.log("开始等待用户登录...")
        start_time = time.time()
        logged_in = False
        
        while time.time() - start_time < timeout_seconds:
            try:
                self.log(f"正在访问 {self.base_url}/chat...")
                self.page.goto(f"{self.base_url}/chat", wait_until="networkidle")
                time.sleep(2)

    def get_stats(self):
        """获取统计信息"""

            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            **self.stats,
            "cache_size": len(self.cache),
            "hit_rate": round(self.stats["cache_hits"] / max(self.stats["total_requests"], 1) * 100, 2)

def get_prompt(template_name: str, **kwargs) -> str:
    """获取指定模板的提示词"""
    template = CHINESE_PROMPT_TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")
    return template.format(**kwargs)

def validate_chinese_response(response: str) -> bool:
    """验证响应是否为有效中文"""
    if not response:
        return False
    # 检查是否包含中文字符
    chinese_chars = sum(1 for c in response if '\u4e00' <= c <= '\u9fff')

def get_prompt(template_name: str, **kwargs) -> str:
    """获取指定模板的提示词"""
    template = CHINESE_PROMPT_TEMPLATES.get(template_name, "")
    return template.format(**kwargs)

    def send_message(self, message: str, wait_time: int = 60) -> str:
        """发送消息并获取回复"""
        try:
            self.log("等待textarea输入框...")
            textarea = self.page.wait_for_selector('textarea')
            self.log("输入消息...")
            textarea.fill(message)
            self.log("按Enter发送...")
            textarea.press('Enter')
            
            self.log("等待回复...")
            time.sleep(3)
